    //dfpSlots is the same param as googletag.pubads().refresh(), it is optional and all slots will be refreshed if it is unspecified.
    function CriteoRefreshDFP(CriteoAdUnits, dfpSlots) {
        var isRefreshAll = ("undefined" == typeof dfpSlots || dfpSlots === null || dfpSlots === '') ? true : false;
        var launchAdServer = function () { googletag.cmd.push(function () { Criteo.SetDFPKeyValueTargeting(); googletag.pubads().refresh(isRefreshAll ? null : dfpSlots); }); }
        Criteo.events.push(function () { Criteo.SetLineItemRanges("0..30:0.01"); Criteo.RequestBids(CriteoAdUnits, launchAdServer, 2000); });
    }

  <script>
   document.onreadystatechange = function () {
        if (document.readyState == "complete") {
            document.querySelector('#caccepted').onclick = function () {
                var dobj = { value: "timeofshowedck", timestamp: new Date().getTime() + (1 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) }
                localStorage.setItem("acc-cookies", JSON.stringify(dobj));
                document.getElementById('cookies-button-container').style.display = 'none';
                return false;
            };
            if (typeof (Storage) !== "undefined") {
                var ckexpd = get_cookie('acc_cookies');
                var week = localStorage.getItem('acc-cookies');
                if (ckexpd == null && week == null && !document.getElementById('trial-topbar-container')) {
                    var ckdate = new Date ( );
                    ckdate.setTime ( ckdate.getTime() + (7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) );//nädal
                    document.cookie = "acc_cookies=;expires=" + ckdate.toGMTString();
                    document.getElementById('cookies-button-container').style.display = 'block';
                };
            };
        };
    };
    function get_cookie(cookie_name) {
        var results = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + cookie_name + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
        if (results)
            return (unescape(results[2]));
        else
            return null;
    };
  </script>

    (function () {
        function loadChartbeat() {
            window._sf_endpt = (new Date()).getTime();
            var e = document.createElement('script');
            e.setAttribute('language', 'javascript');
            e.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript');
            e.setAttribute('src', '//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat_video.js');
            document.body.appendChild(e);
        }
        var oldonload = window.onload;
        window.onload = (typeof window.onload != 'function') ?
            loadChartbeat : function () { oldonload(); loadChartbeat(); };
    })();
  </script>
